<h2 class="kt-adv-heading5518_537ff1-7b wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading5518_537ff1-7b"><strong>Games &amp; Activities</strong></h2>

<h5 class="kt-adv-heading5518_58f19e-50 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color has-theme-palette-2-background-color has-background" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading5518_58f19e-50">Meet the author</h5>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading5518_cdd816-d7 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading5518_cdd816-d7"><strong>Welcome!</strong></h2>



<p style="font-size:18px"><em>I’m Cheryl, and I’m so glad you’re here! When it comes to kids’ art, I’m a super-fan. There’s some­thing so charming about the per­son­al­ity, char­ac­ter, and spon­tane­ity found in the art kids cre­ate.&nbsp;</em></p>



<p style="font-size:18px"><em>After teaching Art to kids from grade K and up for over 20 years, I’m excited to share all I’ve learned with YOU. It’s my passion to help teachers and families share the JOY of ART with the kids in their life. </em></p>



<p class="has-text-align-center"><a href="/about-page/" data-type="page" data-id="79980">Read More</a></p>
</div></div>

					function mgclOnClick() {
						if (!this.target || this.target == '' || this.target == '_self')
							window.location = this.href;
						else
							window.open(this.href,this.target);
						return false;
					}

					// Reduce the number of  conflicting lightboxes
					function mgclAddLoadEvent(func) {
						var oldOnload = window.onload;
						if (typeof window.onload != 'function') {
							window.onload = func;
						} else {
							window.onload = function() {
								oldOnload();
								func();
							}
						}
					}
